name:M‚Äça‚Äçl‚Äçi
info:Discount Twin Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:18 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 28, 2024
msg:Xinxin Hotel is a treasure hotel for my recent business trip and parent-child trip. The hotel itself is located in the West Lake Scenic Area, on Beishan Road, where there are a series of old buildings with a history of a hundred years or more. Most of them are lake-view villas in Western or Chinese and Western styles. The original owners were Zhejiang officials or business tycoons during the National Government period. Now most of them are museums, art galleries, memorial halls or provincial cultural relics. Walking on this street, not only can you see the beautiful scenery of lakes and mountains, but also a strong historical and cultural a**osphere. The reception staff at the front desk of the hotel are very good, professional and thoughtful, with a warm smile. There is also a beautiful lady in the lobby, Guo the foreman, who really answers all the questions of the guests. On the first floor facing the front desk is the 1913 living room, and on the left hand side of the entrance is the 1913 restaurant, which is full at meal times. Our room has a terrace of about 4 square meters, with a little lake view, and the scenery is great. The room is very quiet, the welcome fruit is rich, and free drinks and yogurt are also available. The interior decoration is elegant and nostalgic, with dark green as the main color, which fits well with the herringbone dark brown floor. Sister Yang Xiaolan, who cleaned the room, was very serious and asked repeatedly if there was anything else she needed. She was very enthusiastic and capable. The old-time a**osphere in the room was very consistent with my aesthetics and love, and I took many photos. The "Guyun Caoshe" on the west side of the lobby was lit up at sunset, and the a**osphere was simply beautiful. French food and afternoon tea were provided there. The hotel's breakfast was very rich. If you were lucky, you would be arranged to sit by the window, and the lake view in front of you was a vivid picture. If you plan to come to Hangzhou again in summer and early autumn, Xinxin Hotel will definitely be your best choice next time.
----------------------------------------

msg:Xinxin, with a good geographical location, not only has a long cultural heritage of the Republic of China, but also has a retro and nostalgic decoration style. The lake view room can directly face the West Lake view in the room. Sitting on the bed, you can make a cup of tea with the Nongfu Spring baby water prepared by the store, and enjoy the fruit and cereal yogurt. You can enjoy it in the room, especially the strong misty rain in Jiangnan. Breakfast is in the 1913 restaurant, with a rich variety of Chinese and Western breakfasts. It would be more perfect if the steak was fried freshly. The auntie is also very diligent in cleaning the room. In the afternoon, she will take the initiative to send fruit and water to the room. The toiletries are L'Occitane, baby products are also prepared, and there is a bath set for the bathtub. Uncle Chen's storytelling is the hotel's feature. After breakfast, I waited for Uncle Chen to tell stories. I have a deeper understanding of the hotel and the Republic of China period. I hope the hotel can keep up with the new era. Although there are electric curtains written on the bedside table, they cannot be used. Overall, I feel very satisfied and will continue to choose Xinxin when I come to Hangzhou next time!

msg:Xinxin Hotel is located on the romantic Beishan Road in Hangzhou and has a history spanning two centuries. The design was completed in 1913 and is called "THE NEW HOTEL" in English. The name of the hotel comes from the "Book of Rites¬∑University": "New every day, new every day, new every day" contains the best wishes of "forge ahead"! Some people call it the "Peace Hotel in Hangzhou", while others say it is the "Celebrity Chronicle". Soong Ching Ling, Xu Zhimo, Lu Xun, Lin Huiyin, Zhang Ailing and other half of the celebrities and dignitaries at that time stayed here. I love this Republic of China style! Because the hotel is under renovation, we upgraded the room for free. I love it! 1913 has a good dining environment, good taste, and good service. I even took a group of photos of "flowers" in the evening. It felt great!

msg:When you come to Hangzhou for a rest during the Spring Festival, Xinxin Hotel is the biggest surprise.
The location of the hotel is invincible. The West Lake is right outside the door. Get up early in the morning and take a walk along Beishan Street, and you can walk to Gushan in 10 minutes. On the fourth day of the ***** New Year when there are so many people, you can also get the beautiful view of the empty and quiet West Lake.
The room I stayed in was the Xizi Building Suite, which seemed to be a new type of room opened by the hotel in recent years. It was located in a small annex building between Dongzhuang and Qiushui Mountain Villa. The room is very new, decorated in a new Chinese style, with a record player, an old-fashioned telephone, a teapot and other delicate items, as well as a super rich fruit plate. The focus of the room is obviously the balcony of the bedroom. You can see the beautiful scenery of the West Lake and the lonely mountain under the shade of trees. In addition, the large terrace on the 7th floor of the main building is an excellent spot to overlook the panoramic view of the West Lake!
The breakfast is both Chinese and Western. The Chinese style prefers noodles, and the Western-style baking is very good. There is even a freshly fried steak.
Highly praise the hotel's service! Before I checked in, I was very worried about the parking problem. When I arrived at the hotel, I found that my brother worked very hard, and he could make a parking space for the hotel guests no matter what. When we checked in, we had to wait for the room due to the large number of people during the Spring Festival. The front desk gave us two cups of coffee and asked us to wait in the coffee shop in the lobby. The guy at the front desk is even more powerful. He carried all our luggage and led us to the room. Special thanks to Zhou Meng, the lady at the front desk. We accidentally left a charger behind.
Very satisfied with the whole trip! As a fan of Hu Shi, I hope to live in his celebrity room next time!
The last little suggestion is that it is best to add a lighted vanity mirror in the bathroom for the room type of Xizi Building. The current large mirror is combined with a screen. Although it is smart, the brightness is too low, making it more difficult to put on makeup.

msg:The humidity in Hangzhou in mid-August is very high, and the daytime travel is sultry and unbearable. The stay at Xinxin Hotel is short but comfortable. The 103-year-old building and the superior geographical location give a unique feeling from both the humanities and the landscape. I stayed in a garden-view double room on the 4th floor. The space was not large and the layout was very careful. Living in the "old house" was most worried about the obsolescence and inconvenience of the facilities, but the new hotel did not have this situation at all. Room details such as enough power plugs, Kohler basins, Panasonic bidet, bright light *****s (this is very important), table and chair layout are very new, it can be considered to retain the flavor of the Republic of China, while taking care of the warmth of the details. The staff of the hotel will take the initiative to help push the luggage into the room, especially when he reminds the 7th floor of the landscape platform, the outdoor is sultry and hot, but the view is definitely worth watching. When I left the store, I asked us for advice. I didn't think about it at the time. Now I suggest replacing the hair dryer. The current one is not very easy to use. This is not a flaw, but it can improve the check-in experience!

The welcome fruit has been prepared in the room, and a trace of coolness emerges spontaneously. Choosing Xinxin Hotel, firstly, the hotel has a long history, and celebrities and elegant scholars have stayed there; secondly, the location is very convenient, facing the West Lake, and you can stroll by the lake at any time, especially when the lotus is in full bloom, you will see "the endless green lotus leaves in the sky" in front of you. ", there is the No. 7 bus at the door, and it is also very convenient to go to Lingyin Temple (terminus), Quyuan Fenghe, and Yuewang Temple are also very close. The layout of the hotel is more exquisite, the kettle and the storage box are different from the previous hotels, and the daily fresh language milk is thoughtfully prepared at night. There are many books in the lobby, accompanied by the fragrance of lilies, the cultural heritage and romantic a**osphere quietly permeate. The breakfast is clean, rich, and more Western-style. Of course, there are noodles and wontons. I had dinner at the restaurant of the hotel. Personally, the taste was a little salty, and the price was a little expensive. The hotel is on Beishan Street, the bustling road is easy to be congested, and there are few parking spaces. All in all, I am quite satisfied with my stay this time. It is in line with the reasons for my choice. There should be a next time.
